This adjustment aligns with our growth strategy and aims to entice more price-sensitive consumers.

I underestimated the need for a more aggressive approach given the current competitive landscape.
- **Score:** 5/10

This aligns with my growth strategy and aims to increase our market share significantly.
- **Expected Outcome:** I anticipate an increase in market share to approximately 10-12% and an expected profit increase to around $2 million as the lower rate should attract more borrowers.
